## MCP Integration Guide

### Steps to Complete Integration

1. Implement missing tool schemas from the registry
2. Implement missing tool handlers
3. Update the enhanced_final_mcp_server.py file to include all tools
4. Update the comprehensive_mcp_test.py to test all tools
